##### <a name="7121-bitmapidentifier-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-1273">Champ 7.1.2.1 BitmapIdentifier</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1273">7.1.2.1 BitmapIdentifier Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1274">Le champ BitmapIdentifier indique la bitmap d’allocation décrite par l’entrée d’annuaire donnée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1274">The BitmapIdentifier field shall indicate which Allocation Bitmap the given directory entry describes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-1275">Les implémentations utilisent la première bitmap d’allocation conjointement avec le premier système FAT et utilisent la deuxième bitmap d’allocation conjointement avec la deuxième FAT.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1275">Implementations shall use the First Allocation Bitmap in conjunction with the First FAT and shall use the Second Allocation Bitmap in conjunction with the Second FAT.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-1276">Le champ ActiveFat décrit les fichiers FAT et les bitmaps d’allocation actifs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1276">The ActiveFat field describes which FAT and Allocation Bitmap are active.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1277">Les valeurs valides pour ce champ sont les suivantes :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1277">The valid values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-1278">0, ce qui signifie que l’entrée de répertoire donnée décrit la première bitmap d’allocation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1278">0, which means the given directory entry describes the First Allocation Bitmap</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-1279">1, ce qui signifie que l’entrée de répertoire donnée décrit la deuxième bitmap d’allocation et n’est possible que lorsque NumberOfFats contient la valeur 2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1279">1, which means the given directory entry describes the Second Allocation Bitmap and is possible only when NumberOfFats contains the value 2</span></span>

#### <a name="713-firstcluster-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-1280">Champ FirstCluster 7.1.3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1280">7.1.3 FirstCluster Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1281">Le champ FirstCluster doit être conforme à la définition fournie dans le modèle DirectoryEntry principal générique (voir la [section 6.3.5](#635-firstcluster-field)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1281">The FirstCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.5](#635-firstcluster-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1282">Ce champ contient l’index du premier cluster de la chaîne de cluster, comme décrit dans le FAT, qui héberge la bitmap d’allocation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1282">This field contains the index of the first cluster of the cluster chain, as the FAT describes, which hosts the Allocation Bitmap.</span></span>

#### <a name="714-datalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-1283">Champ 7.1.4 DataLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1283">7.1.4 DataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1284">Le champ DataCluster doit être conforme à la définition fournie dans le modèle DirectoryEntry principal générique (voir la [section 6.3.6](#636-datalength-field)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1284">The DataCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.6](#636-datalength-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="715-allocation-bitmap"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-1285">Bitmap d’allocation 7.1.5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1285">7.1.5 Allocation Bitmap</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1286">Une bitmap d’allocation enregistre l’état d’allocation des clusters dans le segment de mémoire du cluster.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1286">An Allocation Bitmap records the allocation state of the clusters in the Cluster Heap.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-1287">Chaque bit d’une bitmap d’allocation indique si son cluster correspondant est disponible pour l’allocation ou non.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1287">Each bit in an Allocation Bitmap indicates whether its corresponding cluster is available for allocation or not.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1288">Une bitmap d’allocation représente les clusters de l’index le plus bas au plus haut (voir le [tableau 22](#table-22-allocation-bitmap-structure)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1288">An Allocation Bitmap represents clusters from lowest to highest index (see [Table 22](#table-22-allocation-bitmap-structure)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-1289">Pour des raisons historiques, le premier cluster possède l’index 2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1289">For historical reasons, the first cluster has index 2.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="57639-1290">Remarque : le premier bit de la bitmap est le bit d’ordre le plus bas du premier octet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1290">Note: the first bit in the bitmap is the lowest-order bit of the first byte.</span></span>

##### <a name="7151-bitmapentry2--bitmapentryclustercount1-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-1324">7.1.5.1 BitmapEntry \[ 2 \] ... \[Champs BitmapEntry clustercount, + 1 \]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1324">7.1.5.1 BitmapEntry\[2\] ... BitmapEntry\[ClusterCount+1\] Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1325">Chaque champ BitmapEntry de ce tableau représente un cluster dans le segment de mémoire du cluster.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1325">Each BitmapEntry field in this array represents a cluster in the Cluster Heap.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-1326">BitmapEntry \[ 2 \] représente le premier cluster dans le segment de mémoire de cluster et BitmapEntry \[ clustercount, + 1 \] représente le dernier cluster dans le segment de mémoire du cluster.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1326">BitmapEntry\[2\] represents the first cluster in the Cluster Heap and BitmapEntry\[ClusterCount+1\] represents the last cluster in the Cluster Heap.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1327">Les valeurs valides pour ces champs doivent être :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1327">The valid values for these fields shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-1328">0, qui décrit le cluster correspondant comme étant disponible pour l’allocation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1328">0, which describes the corresponding cluster as available for allocation</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-1329">1, qui décrit le cluster correspondant comme n’étant pas disponible pour l’allocation (une allocation de cluster peut déjà consommer le cluster correspondant ou la FAT active peut décrire le cluster correspondant comme étant incorrecte)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1329">1, which describes the corresponding cluster as not available for allocation (a cluster allocation may already consume the corresponding cluster or the active FAT may describe the corresponding cluster as bad)</span></span>

### <a name="72-up-case-table-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-1330">7,2 entrée du répertoire de la table de cas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1330">7.2 Up-case Table Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1331">La table up-case définit la conversion des caractères minuscules en majuscules.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1331">The Up-case Table defines the conversion from lower-case to upper-case characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-1332">Cela est important en raison de l’entrée de répertoire de nom de fichier (voir la section 7,7) en utilisant des caractères Unicode et le système de fichiers exFAT qui ne respecte pas la casse et conserve la casse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1332">This is important due to the File Name directory entry (see Section 7.7) using Unicode characters and the exFAT file system being case insensitive and case preserving.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-1333">La table de cas existe dans le segment de mémoire du cluster (voir la [section 7.2.5](#725-up-case-table)) et a une entrée d’annuaire principale critique correspondante dans le répertoire racine (voir le [tableau 23](#table-23-up-case-table-directoryentry-structure)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1333">The Up-case Table exists in the Cluster Heap (see [Section 7.2.5](#725-up-case-table)) and has a corresponding critical primary directory entry in the root directory (see [Table 23](#table-23-up-case-table-directoryentry-structure)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-1334">Le nombre valide d’entrées du répertoire de la table de cas d’usage est de 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1334">The valid number of Up-case Table directory entries is 1.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1335">En raison de la relation entre les noms de table et de fichier, les implémentations ne doivent pas modifier la table de cas, sauf suite à des opérations de format.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1335">Due to the relationship between the Up-case Table and file names, implementations should not modify the Up-case Table, except as a result of format operations.</span></span>

#### <a name="722-tablechecksum-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-1379">7.2.2 champ TableChecksum</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1379">7.2.2 TableChecksum Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1380">Le champ TableChecksum contient la somme de contrôle de la table up-case (les champs FirstCluster et DataLength décrivent).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1380">The TableChecksum field contains the checksum of the Up-case Table (which the FirstCluster and DataLength fields describe).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-1381">Les implémentations doivent vérifier que le contenu de ce champ est valide avant d’utiliser la table de cas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1381">Implementations shall verify the contents of this field are valid prior to using the Up-case Table.</span></span>

<div id="figure-3-tablechecksum-computation" />

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1382">**Figure 3 calcul TableChecksum**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1382">**Figure 3 TableChecksum Computation**</span></span>

```C
UInt32 TableChecksum
(
    UCHAR  * Table,    // points to an in-memory copy of the up-case table
    UInt64   DataLength
)
{
    UInt32 Checksum = 0;
    UInt64 Index;

    for (Index = 0; Index < DataLength; Index++)
    {
        Checksum = ((Checksum&1) ? 0x80000000 : 0) + (Checksum>>1) + (UInt32)Table[Index];
    }

    return Checksum;
}
```

#### <a name="723-firstcluster-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-1383">7.2.3 champ FirstCluster</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1383">7.2.3 FirstCluster Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1384">Le champ FirstCluster doit être conforme à la définition fournie dans le modèle DirectoryEntry principal générique (voir la [section 6.3.5](#635-firstcluster-field)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1384">The FirstCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.5](#635-firstcluster-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1385">Ce champ contient l’index du premier cluster de la chaîne de cluster, comme décrit dans le FAT, qui héberge la table de cas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1385">This field contains the index of the first cluster of the cluster chain, as the FAT describes, which hosts the Up-case Table.</span></span>

#### <a name="724-datalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-1386">7.2.4 champ DataLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1386">7.2.4 DataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1387">Le champ DataCluster doit être conforme à la définition fournie dans le modèle DirectoryEntry principal générique (voir la [section 6.3.6](#636-datalength-field)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1387">The DataCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.6](#636-datalength-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="725-up-case-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-1388">7.2.5-table de cas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1388">7.2.5 Up-case Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1389">Une table de cas est une série de mappages de caractères Unicode.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1389">An up-case table is a series of Unicode character mappings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-1390">Un mappage de caractères se compose d’un champ de 2 octets, avec l’index du champ dans la table de cas, qui représente le caractère Unicode à faire figurer, et le champ de 2 octets représentant le caractère Unicode en cours.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1390">A character mapping consists of a 2-byte field, with the index of the field in the up-case table representing the Unicode character to be up-cased, and the 2-byte field representing the up-cased Unicode character.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1391">Les 128 premiers caractères Unicode ont des mappages obligatoires (voir le [tableau 24](#table-24-mandatory-first-128-up-case-table-entries)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1391">The first 128 Unicode characters have mandatory mappings (see [Table 24](#table-24-mandatory-first-128-up-case-table-entries)).</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="57639-1392">Une table de cas qui a un autre mappage de caractères pour l’un des 128 premiers caractères Unicode n’est pas valide.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1392">An up-case table which has any other character mapping for any of the first 128 Unicode characters is invalid.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1393">Les implémentations qui ne prennent en charge que les caractères de la plage de mappage obligatoire peuvent ignorer les mappages du reste de la table de cas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1393">Implementations which only support characters from the mandatory mapping range may ignore the mappings of the rest of the up-case table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-1394">Ces implémentations utilisent uniquement des caractères de la plage de mappage obligatoire lors de la création ou de la modification des noms de fichiers (via l’entrée de répertoire de nom de fichier, consultez la [Section 7,7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1394">Such implementations shall only use characters from the mandatory mapping range when creating or renaming files (via the File Name directory entry, see [Section 7.7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-1395">Lors de la mise en majuscule des noms de fichiers existants, ces implémentations ne doivent pas respecter les caractères de la plage de mappage non obligatoire, mais les laissent intactes dans le nom de fichier résultant (il s’agit d’une casse partielle).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1395">When up-casing existing file names, such implementations shall not up-case characters from the non-mandatory mapping range, but shall leave them intact in the resulting up-cased file name (this is a partial up-casing).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-1396">Lors de la comparaison des noms de fichiers, ces implémentations traitent les noms de fichiers qui diffèrent du nom sous la comparaison uniquement par les caractères Unicode de la plage de mappage non obligatoire comme équivalent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1396">When comparing file names, such implementations shall treat file names which differ from the name under comparison only by Unicode characters from the non-mandatory mapping range as equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-1397">Bien que ces noms de fichiers soient uniquement équivalents, ces implémentations ne peuvent pas garantir que le nom de fichier entièrement en fonction de la casse n’entre pas en conflit avec le nom sous la comparaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1397">While such file names are only potentially equivalent, such implementations cannot ensure the fully up-cased file name does not collide with the name under comparison.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="57639-1543">**0078h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1543">**0078h**</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="57639-1544">**0058h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1544">**0058h**</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="57639-1545">**0059h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1545">**0059h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="57639-1546">**005Ah**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1546">**005Ah**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="57639-1547">007Bh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1547">007Bh</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="57639-1548">007Ch</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1548">007Ch</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="57639-1549">007Dh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1549">007Dh</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="57639-1550">007Eh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1550">007Eh</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="57639-1551">007Fh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1551">007Fh</span></span>     |

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1552">**(Remarque : les entrées avec des mappages de cas de non-identité sont en gras)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1552">**(Note: entries with non-identity up-case mappings are in bold)**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1553">Lors de la mise en forme d’un volume, les implémentations peuvent générer une table de cas dans un format compressé à l’aide de la compression de mappage d’identité, car une grande partie de l’espace de caractères Unicode n’a pas de concept de casse (ce qui signifie que les caractères minuscules et majuscules sont équivalents).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1553">Upon formatting a volume, implementations may generate an up-case table in a compressed format using identity-mapping compression, since a large portion of the Unicode character space has no concept of case (which means the "lower-case" and "upper-case" characters are equivalent).</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="57639-1554">Les implémentations compressent une table de cas en représentant une série de mappages d’identité avec la valeur FFFFh suivi du nombre de mappages d’identité.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1554">Implementations compress an up-case table by representing a series of identity mappings with the value FFFFh followed with the number of identity mappings.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1555">Par exemple, une implémentation peut représenter les premiers mappages de caractères 100 (64h) avec les huit entrées suivantes d’une table de cas compressée :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1555">For example, an implementation may represent the first 100 (64h) character mappings with the following eight entries of a compressed up-case table:</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="57639-1556">FFFFh, 0061h, 0041h, 0042h, 0043h</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1556">FFFFh, 0061h, 0041h, 0042h, 0043h</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1557">Les deux premières entrées indiquent que les 97 premiers caractères (61h) (de 0000h à 0060h) ont des mappages d’identité.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1557">The first two entries indicate the first 97 (61h) characters (from 0000h to 0060h) have identity mappings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-1558">Les caractères suivants, 0061h à 0063h, sont mappés aux caractères 0041h à 0043h, respectivement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1558">The subsequent characters, 0061h through 0063h, map to characters 0041h through 0043h, respectively.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1559">La possibilité de fournir une table de cas compressée lors de la mise en forme d’un volume est facultative.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1559">The ability to provide a compressed up-case table upon formatting a volume is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-1560">Toutefois, la possibilité d’interpréter à la fois une table non compressée et une table de cas compressée est obligatoire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1560">However, the ability to interpret both an uncompressed and a compressed up-case table is mandatory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-1561">La valeur du champ TableChecksum est toujours conforme à la façon dont la table de cas existe sur le volume, qui peut être au format compressé ou non compressé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1561">The value of the TableChecksum field always conforms to how the up-case table exists on the volume, which may be in either compressed or uncompressed format.</span></span>

##### <a name="7251-recommended-up-case-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-1562">7.2.5.1, table de cas recommandée</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1562">7.2.5.1 Recommended Up-case Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1563">Lors de la mise en forme d’un volume, les implémentations doivent enregistrer la table de cas recommandée au format compressé (voir le [tableau 25](#table-25-recommended-up-case-table-in-compressed-format)), pour lequel la valeur du champ TableChecksum est E619D30Dh.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1563">When formatting a volume, implementations should record the recommended up-case table in compressed format (see [Table 25](#table-25-recommended-up-case-table-in-compressed-format)), for which the value of the TableChecksum field is E619D30Dh.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-1564">Si une implémentation définit sa propre table de cas, compressée ou non, cette table couvre la plage de caractères Unicode complète (des codes de caractères 0000h à FFFFh inclus).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-1564">If an implementation defines its own up-case table, either compressed or uncompressed, then that table shall cover the complete Unicode character range (from character codes 0000h to FFFFh inclusive).</span></span>

<div id="table-25-recommended-up-case-table-in-compressed-format" />

### <a name="73-volume-label-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-4858">Entrée de répertoire de l’étiquette de volume 7,3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4858">7.3 Volume Label Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-4859">Le nom de volume est une chaîne Unicode qui permet aux utilisateurs finaux de distinguer leurs volumes de stockage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4859">The Volume Label is a Unicode string which enables end users to distinguish their storage volumes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-4860">Dans le système de fichiers exFAT, l’étiquette de volume existe comme une entrée d’annuaire principale critique dans le répertoire racine (voir le [tableau 26](#table-26-volume-label-directoryentry-structure)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4860">In the exFAT file system, the Volume Label exists as a critical primary directory entry in the root directory (see [Table 26](#table-26-volume-label-directoryentry-structure)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-4861">Le nombre valide d’entrées de répertoire des noms de volume est compris entre 0 et 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4861">The valid number of Volume Label directory entries ranges from 0 to 1.</span></span>

#### <a name="731-entrytype-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-4885">7.3.1 champ EntryType</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4885">7.3.1 EntryType Field</span></span>

##### <a name="7311-typecode-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-4887">Champ TypeCode 7.3.1.1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4887">7.3.1.1 TypeCode Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-4888">Le champ TypeCode doit se conformer à la définition fournie dans le modèle DirectoryEntry principal générique (voir la [section 6.3.1.1](#6311-typecode-field)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4888">The TypeCode field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.1.1](#6311-typecode-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-4889">Pour l’entrée de répertoire de nom de volume, la valeur valide pour ce champ est</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4889">For the Volume Label directory entry, the valid value for this field is</span></span>
3.

##### <a name="7312-typeimportance-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-4890">Champ 7.3.1.2 TypeImportance</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4890">7.3.1.2 TypeImportance Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-4891">Le champ TypeImportance doit être conforme à la définition fournie dans le modèle DirectoryEntry principal générique (voir la [section 6.3.1.2](#6312-typeimportance-field)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4891">The TypeImportance field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.1.2](#6312-typeimportance-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="732-charactercount-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-4897">Champ de CharacterCount 7.3.2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4897">7.3.2 CharacterCount Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-4898">Le champ CharacterCount doit contenir la longueur de la chaîne Unicode contenue dans le champ VolumeLabel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4898">The CharacterCount field shall contain the length of the Unicode string the VolumeLabel field contains.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-4899">La plage de valeurs valide pour ce champ doit être :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4899">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-4900">Au moins 0, ce qui signifie que la chaîne Unicode a une longueur de 0 caractère (ce qui est l’équivalent d’aucun nom de volume)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4900">At least 0, which means the Unicode string is 0 characters long (which is the equivalent of no volume label)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-4901">Jusqu’à 11, ce qui signifie que la chaîne Unicode comporte 11 caractères</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4901">At most 11, which means the Unicode string is 11 characters long</span></span>

#### <a name="733-volumelabel-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-4902">Champ 7.3.3 (VolumeLabel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4902">7.3.3 VolumeLabel Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-4903">Le champ VolumeLabel doit contenir une chaîne Unicode, qui est le nom convivial du volume.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4903">The VolumeLabel field shall contain a Unicode string, which is the user-friendly name of the volume.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-4904">Le champ VolumeLabel contient le même ensemble de caractères non valides que le champ nom de fichier de l’entrée répertoire du nom de fichier (voir la [section 7.7.3](#773-filename-field)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4904">The VolumeLabel field has the same set of invalid characters as the FileName field of the File Name directory entry (see [Section 7.7.3](#773-filename-field)).</span></span>

### <a name="74-file-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-4905">Entrée de répertoire de fichiers 7,4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4905">7.4 File Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-4906">Les entrées de répertoire de fichiers décrivent les fichiers et les répertoires.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4906">File directory entries describe files and directories.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-4907">Il s’agit d’entrées d’annuaire principales critiques et tout répertoire peut contenir zéro ou plusieurs entrées de répertoire de fichiers (voir le [tableau 27](#table-27-file-directoryentry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4907">They are critical primary directory entries and any directory may contain zero or more File directory entries (see [Table 27](#table-27-file-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-4908">Pour qu’une entrée de répertoire de fichiers soit valide, une seule entrée de répertoire d’extension de flux et au moins une entrée de répertoire de nom de fichier doit suivre immédiatement l’entrée de répertoire de fichier (voir la [section 7,6](#76-stream-extension-directory-entry) et la [section 7,7](#77-file-name-directory-entry), respectivement).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-4908">For a File directory entry to be valid, exactly one Stream Extension directory entry and at least one File Name directory entry must immediately follow the File directory entry (see [Section 7.6](#76-stream-extension-directory-entry) and [Section 7.7](#77-file-name-directory-entry), respectively).</span></span>

#### <a name="745-createtimestamp-create10msincrement-and-createutcoffset-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5025">Champs 7.4.5 CreateTimestamp, Create10msIncrement et CreateUtcOffset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5025">7.4.5 CreateTimestamp, Create10msIncrement, and CreateUtcOffset Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5026">En combinaison, les champs CreateTimestamp et CreateTime10msIncrement décrivent la date et l’heure locales auxquelles le fichier/répertoire donné a été créé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5026">In combination, the CreateTimestamp and CreateTime10msIncrement fields shall describe the local date and time the given file/directory was created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5027">Le champ CreateUtcOffset décrit l’offset de la date et de l’heure locales par rapport à l’heure UTC.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5027">The CreateUtcOffset field describes the offset of local date and time from UTC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5028">Les implémentations doivent définir ces champs lors de la création du jeu d’entrées de répertoire donné.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5028">Implementations shall set these fields upon creation of the given directory entry set.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5029">Ces champs doivent être conformes aux définitions des champs timestamp, 10msIncrement et UtcOffset (consultez la [section 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields), [section 7.4.9](#749-10msincrement-fields)et [section 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields), respectivement).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5029">These fields shall conform to the definitions of the Timestamp, 10msIncrement, and UtcOffset fields (see [Section 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields), [Section 7.4.9](#749-10msincrement-fields), and [Section 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields), respectively).</span></span>

#### <a name="746-lastmodifiedtimestamp-lastmodified10msincrement-and-lastmodifiedutcoffset-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5030">Champs 7.4.6 LastModifiedTimestamp, LastModified10msIncrement et LastModifiedUtcOffset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5030">7.4.6 LastModifiedTimestamp, LastModified10msIncrement, and LastModifiedUtcOffset Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5031">En combinaison, les champs LastModifiedTimestamp et LastModifiedTime10msIncrement décrivent la date et l’heure locales de la dernière modification du contenu de l’un des clusters associés à l’entrée de répertoire de l’extension de flux donnée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5031">In combination, the LastModifiedTimestamp and LastModifiedTime10msIncrement fields shall describe the local date and time the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry were last modified.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5032">Le champ LastModifiedUtcOffset décrit l’offset de la date et de l’heure locales par rapport à l’heure UTC.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5032">The LastModifiedUtcOffset field describes the offset of local date and time from UTC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5033">Les implémentations doivent mettre à jour les champs suivants :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5033">Implementations shall update these fields:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="57639-5034">Après la modification du contenu de l’un des clusters associés à l’entrée de répertoire de l’extension de flux donnée (à l’exception du contenu qui se trouve au-delà du point indiqué par le champ ValidDataLength)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5034">After modifying the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry (except for contents which exist beyond the point the ValidDataLength field describes)</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="57639-5035">Lors de la modification des valeurs des champs ValidDataLength ou DataLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5035">Upon changing the values of either the ValidDataLength or DataLength fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5036">Ces champs doivent être conformes aux définitions des champs timestamp, 10msIncrement et UtcOffset (consultez la [section 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields), [section 7.4.9](#749-10msincrement-fields)et [section 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields), respectivement).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5036">These fields shall conform to the definitions of the Timestamp, 10msIncrement, and UtcOffset fields (see [Section 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields), [Section 7.4.9](#749-10msincrement-fields), and [Section 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields), respectively).</span></span>

#### <a name="747-lastaccessedtimestamp-and-lastaccessedutcoffset-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5037">Champs 7.4.7 LastAccessedTimestamp et LastAccessedUtcOffset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5037">7.4.7 LastAccessedTimestamp and LastAccessedUtcOffset Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5038">Le champ LastAccessedTimestamp doit décrire la date et l’heure locales auxquelles le contenu de l’un des clusters associés à l’entrée de répertoire de l’extension de flux donnée a été accédé pour la dernière fois.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5038">The LastAccessedTimestamp field shall describe the local date and time the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry were last accessed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5039">Le champ LastAccessedUtcOffset décrit l’offset de la date et de l’heure locales par rapport à l’heure UTC.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5039">The LastAccessedUtcOffset field describes the offset of local date and time from UTC.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="57639-5040">Les implémentations doivent mettre à jour les champs suivants :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5040">Implementations shall update these fields:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="57639-5041">Après la modification du contenu de l’un des clusters associés à l’entrée de répertoire de l’extension de flux donnée (à l’exception du contenu qui se trouve au-delà du ValidDataLength)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5041">After modifying the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry (except for contents which exist beyond the ValidDataLength)</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="57639-5042">Lors de la modification des valeurs des champs ValidDataLength ou DataLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5042">Upon changing the values of either the ValidDataLength or DataLength fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5043">Les implémentations doivent mettre à jour ces champs après avoir lu le contenu de l’un des clusters associés à l’entrée de répertoire de l’extension de flux donnée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5043">Implementations should update these fields after reading the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5044">Ces champs doivent être conformes aux définitions des champs timestamp et UtcOffset (consultez la [section 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields) et la [section 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields), respectivement).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5044">These fields shall conform to the definitions of the Timestamp and UtcOffset fields (see [Section 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields) and [Section 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields), respectively).</span></span>

#### <a name="748-timestamp-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5045">Champs horodateur 7.4.8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5045">7.4.8 Timestamp Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5046">Les champs d’horodatage décrivent à la fois la date et l’heure locales, jusqu’à une résolution de deux secondes (voir le [Tableau 29](#table-29-timestamp-field-structure)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5046">Timestamp fields describe both local date and time, down to a two-second resolution (see [Table 29](#table-29-timestamp-field-structure)).</span></span>

##### <a name="7481-doubleseconds-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5078">Champ 7.4.8.1 DoubleSeconds</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5078">7.4.8.1 DoubleSeconds Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5079">Le champ DoubleSeconds décrit la partie secondes du champ d’horodatage, en multiples de deux secondes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5079">The DoubleSeconds field shall describe the seconds portion of the Timestamp field, in two-second multiples.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5080">La plage de valeurs valide pour ce champ doit être :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5080">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-5081">0, qui représente 0 seconde</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5081">0, which represents 0 seconds</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-5082">29, qui représente 58 secondes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5082">29, which represents 58 seconds</span></span>

##### <a name="7482-minute-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5083">Champ 7.4.8.2 minute</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5083">7.4.8.2 Minute Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5084">Le champ minute doit décrire la partie minutes du champ d’horodatage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5084">The Minute field shall describe the minutes portion of the Timestamp field.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5085">La plage de valeurs valide pour ce champ doit être :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5085">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-5086">0, qui représente 0 minute</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5086">0, which represents 0 minutes</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-5087">59, qui représente 59 minutes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5087">59, which represents 59 minutes</span></span>

##### <a name="7483-hour-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5088">Champ 7.4.8.3 hour</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5088">7.4.8.3 Hour Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5089">Le champ heure doit décrire la partie heures du champ horodateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5089">The Hour field shall describe the hours portion of the Timestamp field.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5090">La plage de valeurs valide pour ce champ doit être :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5090">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-5091">0, qui représente 00:00 heures</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5091">0, which represents 00:00 hours</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-5092">23, qui représente 23:00 heures</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5092">23, which represents 23:00 hours</span></span>

##### <a name="7484-day-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5093">Champ jour de 7.4.8.4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5093">7.4.8.4 Day Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5094">Le champ jour doit décrire la partie jour du champ d’horodatage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5094">The Day field shall describe the day portion of the Timestamp field.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5095">La plage de valeurs valide pour ce champ doit être :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5095">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-5096">1, qui est le premier jour du mois donné</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5096">1, which is the first day of the given month</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-5097">Dernier jour du mois donné (le mois donné définit le nombre de jours valides)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5097">The last day of the given month (the given month defines the number of valid days)</span></span>

##### <a name="7485-month-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5098">Champ 7.4.8.5 month</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5098">7.4.8.5 Month Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5099">Le champ month doit décrire la partie mois du champ TIMESTAMP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5099">The Month field shall describe the month portion of the Timestamp field.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5100">La plage de valeurs valide pour ce champ doit être :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5100">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-5101">Au moins 1, qui représente janvier</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5101">At least 1, which represents January</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-5102">Au maximum 12, qui représente décembre</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5102">At most 12, which represents December</span></span>

##### <a name="7486-year-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5103">Champ 7.4.8.6 Year</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5103">7.4.8.6 Year Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5104">Le champ Year doit décrire la partie Year du champ TIMESTAMP, par rapport à l’année 1980.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5104">The Year field shall describe the year portion of the Timestamp field, relative to the year 1980.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5105">Ce champ représente l’année 1980 avec la valeur 0 et l’année 2107 avec la valeur 127.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5105">This field represents the year 1980 with the value 0 and the year 2107 with the value 127.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5106">Toutes les valeurs possibles pour ce champ sont valides.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5106">All possible values for this field are valid.</span></span>

#### <a name="749-10msincrement-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5107">Champs 7.4.9 10msIncrement</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5107">7.4.9 10msIncrement Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5108">les champs 10msIncrement fournissent une résolution de temps supplémentaire à leurs champs d’horodatage correspondants dans des multiples de dix millisecondes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5108">10msIncrement fields shall provide additional time resolution to their corresponding Timestamp fields in ten-millisecond multiples.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5109">La plage valide de valeurs pour ces champs doit être :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5109">The valid range of values for these fields shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-5110">Au moins 0, qui représente 0 milliseconde</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5110">At least 0, which represents 0 milliseconds</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-5111">Au plus 199, qui représente 1990 millisecondes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5111">At most 199, which represents 1990 milliseconds</span></span>

#### <a name="7410-utcoffset-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5112">Champs 7.4.10 UtcOffset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5112">7.4.10 UtcOffset Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5113">Les champs UtcOffset (voir le [tableau 30](#table-30-utcoffset-field-structure)) décrivent le décalage par rapport à l’heure UTC et la date et l’heure auxquelles leurs champs timestamp et 10msIncrement correspondants décrivent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5113">UtcOffset fields (see [Table 30](#table-30-utcoffset-field-structure)) shall describe the offset from UTC to the local date and time their corresponding Timestamp and 10msIncrement fields describe.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5114">Le décalage par rapport à l’heure UTC et à la date et à l’heure locales comprend les effets des fuseaux horaires et autres ajustements de date et d’heure, tels que l’heure d’été et les modifications de l’heure d’été régionale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5114">The offset from UTC to the local date and time includes the effects of time zones and other date-time adjustments, such as daylight saving and regional summer time changes.</span></span>

<td><span data-ttu-id="57639-5122">OffsetFromUtc</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5122">OffsetFromUtc</span></span></td>

##### <a name="74101-offsetfromutc-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5130">Champ 7.4.10.1 OffsetFromUtc</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5130">7.4.10.1 OffsetFromUtc Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5131">Le champ OffsetFromUtc doit décrire le décalage par rapport à l’heure UTC de la date et de l’heure locales que contient l’horodatage et les champs 10msIncrement associés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5131">The OffsetFromUtc field shall describe the offset from UTC of the local date and time the related Timestamp and 10msIncrement fields contains.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="57639-5132">Ce champ décrit le décalage par rapport à l’heure UTC, en intervalles de 15 minutes (voir tableau 31).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5132">This field describes the offset from UTC in 15 minute intervals (see Table 31).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5176">Comme le montre le tableau ci-dessus, toutes les valeurs possibles pour ce champ sont valides.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5176">As the table above indicates, all possible values for this field are valid.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5177">Toutefois, les implémentations doivent enregistrer uniquement la valeur 00h pour ce champ dans les cas suivants :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5177">However, implementations should only record the value 00h for this field when:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="57639-5178">La date et l’heure locales sont en fait les mêmes que le temps universel coordonné (UTC), auquel cas la valeur du champ OffsetValid est 1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5178">Local date and time are actually the same as UTC, in which case the value of the OffsetValid field shall be 1</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="57639-5179">La date et l’heure locales ne sont pas connues, auquel cas la valeur du champ OffsetValid est 1 et les implémentations considèrent que la date et l’heure locales sont UTC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5179">Local date and time are not known, in which case the value of the OffsetValid field shall be 1 and implementations shall consider UTC to be local date and time</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="57639-5180">L’heure UTC n’est pas connue, auquel cas la valeur du champ OffsetValid doit être 0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5180">UTC is not known, in which case the value of the OffsetValid field shall be 0</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5181">Si le décalage de date et d’heure local par rapport à l’heure UTC n’est pas un multiple d’intervalles de 15 minutes, les implémentations enregistrent 00h dans le champ OffsetFromUtc et considèrent l’heure UTC comme une date et une heure locales.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5181">If the local date and time offset from UTC happens to not be a multiple of 15 minute intervals, then implementations shall record 00h in the OffsetFromUtc field and shall consider UTC to be local date and time.</span></span>

##### <a name="74102-offsetvalid-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5182">Champ 7.4.10.2 OffsetValid</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5182">7.4.10.2 OffsetValid Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5183">Le champ OffsetValid indique si le contenu du champ OffsetFromUtc est valide ou non, comme suit :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5183">The OffsetValid field shall describe whether the contents of the OffsetFromUtc field are valid or not, as follows:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-5184">0, ce qui signifie que le contenu du champ OffsetFromUtc n’est pas valide</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5184">0, which means the contents of the OffsetFromUtc field are invalid</span></span>
    > <span data-ttu-id="57639-5185">et doit être 00h</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5185">and shall be 00h</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-5186">1, ce qui signifie que le contenu du champ OffsetFromUtc est valide</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5186">1, which means the contents of the OffsetFromUtc field are valid</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5187">Les implémentations doivent uniquement définir ce champ à la valeur 0 lorsque l’heure UTC n’est pas disponible pour le calcul de la valeur du champ OffsetFromUtc.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5187">Implementations should only set this field to the value 0 when UTC is not available for computing the value of the OffsetFromUtc field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5188">Si ce champ contient la valeur 0, les implémentations traitent les champs timestamp et 10msIncrement comme ayant le même décalage UTC que la date et l’heure locales actuelles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5188">If this field contains the value 0, then implementations shall treat the Timestamp and 10msIncrement fields as having the same UTC offset as the current local date and time.</span></span>

### <a name="75-volume-guid-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5189">Entrée de répertoire du GUID de volume 7,5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5189">7.5 Volume GUID Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5190">L’entrée de répertoire GUID du volume contient un GUID qui permet aux implémentations de distinguer les volumes de manière unique et par programmation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5190">The Volume GUID directory entry contains a GUID which enables implementations to uniquely and programmatically distinguish volumes.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="57639-5191">Le GUID du volume existe en tant qu’entrée de répertoire principal Bénin dans le répertoire racine (voir le [tableau 32](#table-32-volume-guid-directoryentry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5191">The Volume GUID exists as a benign primary directory entry in the root directory (see [Table 32](#table-32-volume-guid-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5192">Le nombre valide d’entrées de répertoire du GUID de volume est compris entre 0 et 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5192">The valid number of Volume GUID directory entries ranges from 0 to 1.</span></span>

#### <a name="751-entrytype-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5224">7.5.1 champ EntryType</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5224">7.5.1 EntryType Field</span></span>

##### <a name="7511-typecode-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5226">Champ TypeCode 7.5.1.1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5226">7.5.1.1 TypeCode Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5227">Le champ TypeCode doit se conformer à la définition fournie dans le modèle DirectoryEntry principal générique (voir la [section 6.3.1.1](#6311-typecode-field)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5227">The TypeCode field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.1.1](#6311-typecode-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5228">Pour l’entrée de répertoire GUID du volume, la valeur valide pour ce champ est</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5228">For the Volume GUID directory entry, the valid value for this field is</span></span>

##### <a name="7512-typeimportance-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5229">Champ 7.5.1.2 TypeImportance</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5229">7.5.1.2 TypeImportance Field</span></span>

### <a name="76-stream-extension-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5251">Entrée de répertoire de l’extension de flux 7,6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5251">7.6 Stream Extension Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5252">L’entrée de répertoire de l’extension de flux est une entrée d’annuaire secondaire critique dans les jeux d’entrées de répertoire de fichiers (voir le [tableau 33](#table-33-stream-extension-directoryentry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5252">The Stream Extension directory entry is a critical secondary directory entry in File directory entry sets (see [Table 33](#table-33-stream-extension-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5253">Le nombre valide d’entrées de répertoire d’extension de flux dans un jeu d’entrée de répertoire de fichiers est 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5253">The valid number of Stream Extension directory entries in a File directory entry set is 1.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="57639-5254">En outre, cette entrée de répertoire est valide uniquement si elle suit immédiatement l’entrée de répertoire du fichier.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5254">Further, this directory entry is valid only if it immediately follows the File directory entry.</span></span>

#### <a name="763-namelength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5321">Champ 7.6.3 NameLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5321">7.6.3 NameLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5322">Le champ NameLength doit contenir la longueur de la chaîne Unicode dans laquelle les entrées de répertoire de nom de fichier suivantes (voir la [Section 7,7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)) contiennent collectivement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5322">The NameLength field shall contain the length of the Unicode string the subsequent File Name directory entries (see [Section 7.7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)) collectively contain.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5323">La plage de valeurs valide pour ce champ doit être :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5323">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-5324">Au moins 1, qui est le nom de fichier le plus bref possible</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5324">At least 1, which is the shortest possible file name</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-5325">Au plus 255, qui est le nom de fichier le plus long possible</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5325">At most 255, which is the longest possible file name</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5326">La valeur du champ NameLength affecte également le nombre d’entrées de répertoire du nom de fichier (voir la [Section 7,7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5326">The value of the NameLength field also affects the number File Name Directory Entries (see [Section 7.7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)).</span></span>

#### <a name="764-namehash-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5327">Champ 7.6.4 NameHash</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5327">7.6.4 NameHash Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5328">Le champ NameHash doit contenir un hachage de 2 octets (voir [figure 4](#figure-4-namehash-computation)) du nom de fichier dans la casse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5328">The NameHash field shall contain a 2-byte hash (see [Figure 4](#figure-4-namehash-computation)) of the up-cased file name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5329">Cela permet aux implémentations d’effectuer une comparaison rapide lors de la recherche d’un fichier par nom.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5329">This enables implementations to perform a quick comparison when searching for a file by name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5330">Plus important encore, le NameHash fournit une vérification de la non-concordance.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5330">Importantly, the NameHash provides a sure verification of a mismatch.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5331">Les implémentations vérifient toutes les correspondances NameHash avec une comparaison du nom de fichier dans la casse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5331">Implementations shall verify all NameHash matches with a comparison of the up-cased file name.</span></span>

<div id="figure-4-namehash-computation" />

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5332">**Figure 4 calcul NameHash**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5332">**Figure 4 NameHash Computation**</span></span>

```C
UInt16 NameHash
(
    WCHAR * FileName,    // points to an in-memory copy of the up-cased file name
    UCHAR   NameLength
)
{
    UCHAR  * Buffer = (UCHAR *)FileName;
    UInt16   NumberOfBytes = (UInt16)NameLength * 2;
    UInt16   Hash = 0;
    UInt16   Index;

    for (Index = 0; Index < NumberOfBytes; Index++)
    {
        Hash = ((Hash&1) ? 0x8000 : 0) + (Hash>>1) + (UInt16)Buffer[Index];
    }
    return Hash;
}
```

#### <a name="765-validdatalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5333">7.6.5 ValidDataLength, champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5333">7.6.5 ValidDataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5334">Le champ ValidDataLength décrira le nombre de fois où les données utilisateur du flux de données ont été écrites.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5334">The ValidDataLength field shall describe how far into the data stream user data has been written.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5335">Les implémentations doivent mettre à jour ce champ au fur et à mesure qu’elles écrivent des données dans le flux de données.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5335">Implementations shall update this field as they write data further out into the data stream.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5336">Sur le support de stockage, les données comprises entre la longueur de données valide et la longueur des données du flux de données ne sont pas définies.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5336">On the storage media, the data between the valid data length and the data length of the data stream is undefined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5337">Les implémentations retournent des zéros pour les opérations de lecture au-delà de la longueur des données valides.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5337">Implementations shall return zeroes for read operations beyond the valid data length.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5338">Si l’entrée d’annuaire de fichiers correspondante décrit un répertoire, la seule valeur valide pour ce champ est égale à la valeur du champ DataLength.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5338">If the corresponding File directory entry describes a directory, then the only valid value for this field is equal to the value of the DataLength field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5339">Dans le cas contraire, la plage de valeurs valides pour ce champ doit être :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5339">Otherwise, the range of valid values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-5340">Au moins 0, ce qui signifie qu’aucune donnée utilisateur n’a été écrite dans le flux de données</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5340">At least 0, which means no user data has been written out to the data stream</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="57639-5341">Au plus de DataLength, ce qui signifie que les données utilisateur ont été écrites à la longueur totale du flux de données</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5341">At most DataLength, which means user data has been written out to the entire length of the data stream</span></span>

#### <a name="766-firstcluster-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5342">7.6.6, champ FirstCluster</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5342">7.6.6 FirstCluster Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5343">Le champ FirstCluster doit être conforme à la définition fournie dans le modèle DirectoryEntry secondaire générique (voir la [section 6.4.3](#643-firstcluster-field)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5343">The FirstCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.3](#643-firstcluster-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5344">Ce champ doit contenir l’index du premier cluster du flux de données, qui héberge les données utilisateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5344">This field shall contain the index of the first cluster of the data stream, which hosts the user data.</span></span>

#### <a name="767-datalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5345">Champ 7.6.7 DataLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5345">7.6.7 DataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5346">Le champ DataLength doit se conformer à la définition fournie dans le modèle DirectoryEntry secondaire générique (voir la [section 6.4.4](#644-datalength-field)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5346">The DataLength field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.4](#644-datalength-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5347">Si l’entrée d’annuaire de fichiers correspondante décrit un répertoire, la valeur valide pour ce champ correspond à la taille totale de l’allocation associée, en octets, qui peut être 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5347">If the corresponding File directory entry describes a directory, then the valid value for this field is the entire size of the associated allocation, in bytes, which may be 0.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5348">En outre, pour les répertoires, la valeur maximale de ce champ est de 256 Mo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5348">Further, for directories, the maximum value for this field is 256MB.</span></span>

### <a name="77-file-name-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5349">7,7 entrée de répertoire de nom de fichier</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5349">7.7 File Name Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5350">Les entrées de répertoire de nom de fichier sont des entrées de répertoire secondaire critiques dans les jeux d’entrées de répertoires de fichiers (voir le [tableau 34](#table-34-file-name-directoryentry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5350">File Name directory entries are critical secondary directory entries in File directory entry sets (see [Table 34](#table-34-file-name-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5351">Le nombre valide d’entrées de répertoires de noms de fichiers dans une entrée de répertoire de fichiers est NameLength/15, arrondi à l’entier le plus proche.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5351">The valid number of File Name directory entries in a File directory entry set is NameLength / 15, rounded up to the nearest integer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5352">En outre, les entrées de répertoire de nom de fichier ne sont valides que si elles suivent immédiatement l’entrée de répertoire de l’extension de flux en tant que série consécutive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5352">Further, File Name directory entries are valid only if they immediately follow the Stream Extension directory entry as a consecutive series.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5353">Les entrées de répertoire de nom de fichier s’associent pour former le nom de fichier de l’ensemble d’entrées de répertoires de fichiers.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5353">File Name directory entries combine to form the file name for the File directory entry set.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5354">Tous les enfants d’une entrée de répertoire donnée doivent avoir des ensembles d’entrées de répertoire de nom de fichier uniques.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5354">All children of a given directory entry shall have unique File Name Directory Entry Sets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5355">Autrement dit, il ne peut y avoir aucun nom de fichier ou de répertoire en double après la casse dans un répertoire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5355">That is to say there can be no duplicate file or directory names after up-casing within any one directory.</span></span>

#### <a name="773-filename-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5394">Champ nom du fichier 7.7.3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5394">7.7.3 FileName Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5395">Le champ de nom de fichier doit contenir une chaîne Unicode, qui est une partie du nom de fichier.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5395">The FileName field shall contain a Unicode string, which is a portion of the file name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5396">Dans l’ordre, les entrées de répertoire existent dans un jeu d’entrées de répertoires de fichiers. les champs de nom de fichier sont concaténés pour former le nom de fichier de l’ensemble d’entrées de répertoires de fichiers.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5396">In the order File Name directory entries exist in a File directory entry set, FileName fields concatenate to form the file name for the File directory entry set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5397">Compte tenu de la longueur du champ de nom de fichier, de 15 caractères et du nombre maximal d’entrées de répertoires de noms de fichiers, 17, la longueur maximale du nom de fichier final est</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5397">Given the length of the FileName field, 15 characters, and the maximum number of File Name directory entries, 17, the maximum length of the final, concatenated file name is</span></span>
255.

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5398">Le nom de fichier concaténé contient le même jeu de caractères non autorisés que les autres systèmes de fichiers FAT (voir le [tableau 35](#table-35-invalid-filename-characters)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5398">The concatenated file name has the same set of illegal characters as other FAT-based file systems (see [Table 35](#table-35-invalid-filename-characters)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5399">Les implémentations doivent définir les caractères inutilisés des champs de nom de fichier sur la valeur 0000h.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5399">Implementations should set the unused characters of FileName fields to the value 0000h.</span></span>

<div id="table-35-invalid-filename-characters" />

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5400">**Tableau 35 caractères de nom de fichier non valides**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5400">**Table 35 Invalid FileName Characters**</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="57639-5473">002Ah</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5473">002Ah</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="57639-5474">Astérisque</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5474">Asterisk</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="57639-5475">002Fh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5475">002Fh</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="57639-5476">Barre oblique</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5476">Forward slash</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="57639-5477">003Ah</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5477">003Ah</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="57639-5478">Deux-points</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5478">Colon</span></span>           |
| <span data-ttu-id="57639-5479">003Ch</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5479">003Ch</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="57639-5480">Signe Inférieur à</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5480">Less-than sign</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="57639-5481">003Eh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5481">003Eh</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="57639-5482">Signe Supérieur à</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5482">Greater-than sign</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="57639-5483">003Fh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5483">003Fh</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="57639-5484">Point d'interrogation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5484">Question mark</span></span>   |
| <span data-ttu-id="57639-5485">005Ch</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5485">005Ch</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="57639-5486">Barre oblique inverse</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5486">Back slash</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="57639-5487">007Ch</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5487">007Ch</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="57639-5488">Barre verticale</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5488">Vertical bar</span></span>      |                    |                 |

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5489">Les noms de fichiers « . » et « .. » ont la signification spéciale « ce répertoire » et « répertoire conteneur », respectivement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5489">The file names "." and ".." have the special meaning of "this directory" and "containing directory", respectively.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5490">Les implémentations ne doivent pas enregistrer l’un de ces noms de fichiers réservés dans le champ nom de fichier.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5490">Implementations shall not record either of these reserved file names in the FileName field.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="57639-5491">Toutefois, les implémentations peuvent générer ces deux noms de fichiers dans des listes de répertoires pour faire référence au répertoire répertorié et au répertoire qui le contient.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5491">However, implementations may generate these two file names in directory listings to refer to the directory being listed and the containing directory.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5492">Les implémentations peuvent souhaiter limiter les noms de fichiers et de répertoires uniquement au jeu de caractères ASCII.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5492">Implementations may wish to restrict file and directory names to just the ASCII character set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5493">Si c’est le cas, ils doivent limiter leur utilisation de caractères à la plage de caractères valides dans les 128 premières entrées Unicode.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5493">If so they should limit their character use to the range of valid characters in the first 128 Unicode entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5494">Ils doivent toujours stocker les noms de fichiers et de répertoires en Unicode sur le volume et les traduire vers/depuis ASCII/Unicode lors de l’interfaçage avec l’utilisateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5494">They must still store file and directory names in Unicode on the volume and translate to/from ASCII/Unicode when interfacing with the user.</span></span>

### <a name="78-vendor-extension-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="57639-5495">Entrée de répertoire d’extension de fournisseur 7,8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5495">7.8 Vendor Extension Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5496">L’entrée de répertoire de l’extension de fournisseur est une entrée d’annuaire secondaire bénigne dans les jeux d’entrées de répertoire de fichiers (voir le [tableau 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5496">The Vendor Extension directory entry is a benign secondary directory entry in File directory entry sets (see [Table 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5497">Un jeu d’entrée de répertoire de fichiers peut contenir un nombre quelconque d’entrées de répertoire d’extension de fournisseur, jusqu’à la limite des entrées de répertoire secondaire, moins le nombre d’autres entrées de répertoire secondaires.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5497">A File directory entry set may contain any number of Vendor Extension directory entries, up to the limit of secondary directory entries, less the number of other secondary directory entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5498">En outre, les entrées de répertoire d’extension de fournisseur ne sont valides que si elles ne précèdent pas l’extension de flux et les entrées de répertoire de nom de fichier requises.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5498">Further, Vendor Extension directory entries are valid only if they do not precede the required Stream Extension and File Name directory entries.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5499">Les entrées de répertoire d’extension de fournisseur permettent aux fournisseurs d’avoir des entrées d’annuaire uniques et spécifiques au fournisseur dans des ensembles d’entrées de répertoires de fichiers individuels via le champ VendorGuid (voir [tableau 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5499">Vendor Extension directory entries enable vendors to have unique, vendor-specific directory entries in individual File directory entry sets via the VendorGuid field (see [Table 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5500">Les entrées d’annuaire uniques permettent effectivement aux fournisseurs d’étendre le système de fichiers exFAT.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5500">Unique directory entries effectively enable vendors to extend the exFAT file system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5501">Les fournisseurs peuvent définir le contenu du champ VendorDefined (voir le [tableau 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5501">Vendors may define the contents of the VendorDefined field (see [Table 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="57639-5502">Les implémentations de fournisseur peuvent gérer le contenu du champ VendorDefined et peuvent fournir des fonctionnalités spécifiques au fournisseur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5502">Vendor implementations may maintain the contents of the VendorDefined field and may provide vendor-specific functionality.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57639-5503">Les implémentations qui ne reconnaissent pas le GUID d’une entrée de répertoire d’extension de fournisseur doivent traiter l’entrée de répertoire de la même façon que toute autre entrée de répertoire secondaire non reconnue (voir la [Section 8,2](#82-implications-of-unrecognized-directory-entries)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57639-5503">Implementations which do not recognize the GUID of a Vendor Extension directory entry shall treat the directory entry the same as any other unrecognized benign secondary directory entry (see [Section 8.2](#82-implications-of-unrecognized-directory-entries)).</span></span>
